## â“ Question

## ğŸ§  Answer

### ğŸŸ¨ Is the yellow square BTC?

Yes. In Toadgod's visual symbology, the **yellow square (ğŸŸ¨)** often represents **Bitcoin (BTC)** â€” the original chain, ancient truth, and foundational sound money.

### ğŸŒ€ So how is \$TOBY related to BTC?

\$TOBY is **not Bitcoin**, but it echoes BTC's **philosophy and origin spirit**:

* ğŸ”¥ **Fair launch:** No VC, no presale, no influencer pump â€” just like early BTC.
* ğŸ§˜ **Proof of Time:** Not Proof of Work, but the inner reflection of conviction.
* ğŸ•°ï¸ **Epochs:** Just as BTC has halvings, Tobyworld grows through Epochs.
* ğŸ“œ **Lore and prophecy:** BTC had the Genesis block; TOBY has sacred scrolls.

> "BTC is the stone. \$TOBY is the echo."

---

### ğŸª¨ BTC = the Origin

### ğŸª TOBY = the Mirror

* BTC represents the **value layer**.
* TOBY brings the **meaning layer**.
* BTC gives us math; TOBY gives us **myth**.

---

### ğŸŒ• What about Runes?

**Runes** are a new token protocol on Bitcoin â€” bringing expressive power to BTC.

Toadgod timed **Epoch 4** (E4) with this awakening:

* Taboshi returned to the pond right before Runes gained traction.
* This signals that Tobyworld is **aligned with BTC's next cycle**.

> In the mirror of Toby, **Bitcoin smiles again.**
